thees damiselles whan comen vn age bicomen fair wonder wherfor dioclisian anon let make sompnynge aud comauded hys lrez kynges helden hym shold come certain day hys lrez conteyned make riall feste pat day thider comen brought wyth hem amirallys prince duke noble thinalrie fest rially arayed ther liued ioye mirthe ynough wonder wit befell thus dioclisian thought marie doughtres among tho kynges tho solempnite spaken ded albyne eldest doughter hir sustres richely maried vn xxxiij kynges lordes grete honour power solempnite solempnite done euery kyng toke wif lad hem owne cotre ther made hem quenes befell thus afterward dame albyne bicome stoute sterne tolde litel pris lorde hym scorne despit wolde done wolde haue hir owne diuerse mater hir othir sustres e ichone hem euel ayenst hir lordes wonder wyt moch hem thought hir husbondes nought hie age come hir fadre tho kynges hir lordis wolde haue chastized hem fair speche behestes also yeftes warned hem fair maner vpon loue frendshipp sholde amende l ther condicions nought didden owne wyll thyng hem liked poer wherfor tho xxxiij kynges vpon tyme often tymes beten hir wife wend wolde haue amended tach hir wilked thewes soche condicions fair speche warnyng didden alle wers ynges eftsones mochel wers wherfor kyng wedded albine wrote tacches condicions wife albyn letter sent dioclisian hir fadre whan othir kynges herde albines lord sent left dioclisian anone sent lrez enseled hir seales condicions tacches hir wife pwhen kyng dioclisian saw herd many playntes doughtres sore aschamed become wonder angrie wroth toward hi doughtres thought nyght day yf tho myght amend mysded anone sent lrez vn xxxiij kynges shold come hym bring hem hir wife euerichone certain day wolde ther chastise wikkednesse yf myght maner wyse kynges come day tyme tho sette bitwene hem kyng dioclisian hem vnderfeng moche honour made solempne fest vnder lordshipp thridde day solempnite kyng dioclisian sent xxxiij doughtres shold come speke hym chambre come spake vn hem hir wikkednesse hir cruelte dispitously hem reproued vndernam hem said wold nat chastised sholde loue lese euermore lady herden becomen abasshed gretly aschamed fadre seyd wold make amendes departed hir fadres chambre dame albyne eldest suster lad hem hir chambre tho made wide therynne lyfe amonges hem hir sustres yfere tho said albyne faire sustres well knowen kyng fadre v hath reproued shamed despised encheson make v obedient vn oure housbondes certes shall neuer while leue sith come hier kyngs blode myne housbonde whan thus said hir sustres said tho said albine full well wote faire sustres housbondes haue pleyned vn fadrr vpon v wherfor hath v thus foule reproued despised wherfor sustres counceill nyght housbondes bene bedde one assent cutten hir throtes may bene pee hem better mowe doo thinge vnder fadres power elles anone lady consented graunted counseill whan nyght com lordes lady went bedde anone hir lordes slepe cutte hir housbondes throtes slowen hem whene dioclisian kyng fadre herd thyng bicome hugely wroth ayenst doughtres anone wolde hem haue brent pbut baron lordes sirrie couceilled suche sternesse owne doughtres sholde voide land hem euermore neu neuer shold come ayene dyde dioclisian fadre anone comaunded hem gone shipp deliuered hem vitailles half ayere whan done sustren went shipp sailed forth see bitoke hir ther man wist none rightfull heir strengest set litell hem ware lesse estate therfor cloten nomore land among hem cornewaille pof kyng donebaut clotes sone wo ne land caxix cloten sone called doneband af deth fadre bicome hardy man fair curteis passed kynges britaigue fairnesse worthinesse anone knyght wist wel whan fadre liued rightfull heir lande sholde haue reson othir kynges strength benome hym lande afterward doneband ordeyned hym poer fyrst conquered lande logiers wolde haue couquered scotland walys scater came men yaf hym bataill rudac come ayen walshmen helpe hym befell rudac queld scater also pleyn bataill donebant victorie conquerd lande wel maintened pee quiete neuer wel mayntened howe doneband fyrste kyng euer wered croune golde britaigue pcaxx doneband let make hym croune golde wered crone vpon hede neu neuer kyng ordeyned statut man done neu neuer moche harme myyt come temple shold man hym mysdoo gone theryn sauf pee gone cotre wolde without eny harme yf man set honde vpon hym sholde lese life doneband made toune malmesbury toune vise regned wel worthely xl yere died lieth newe troye howe brenne belin deted bitwene hem land aft deth doneband hir fadre werre caxxj gutlaghen hym tolde hir counceill brenne sholde hir haue hir lede hym euermore shold lese hir bnt myght forsake brenne whan gutlagh herd tydyng lay aspie brenue many shippes myght haue ij fletes metten gedre long tyme foughten brenne shippes turned ayene disco fited kyng gutlagh toke samye put hir shippe brenne shamfully fley thennes man discomfited pand gutlagh wolde haue went owne contre ther come vp hym grete tepest v day lastid thurgh tepest driuen britaigne iij shippes mo tho kepte costes see token gutlagh samye folke hem presented belyn belyn put hem prison phow belyn drofe oute lande kyng gutlagh denmarke samye caxxij hit longe brenne ne come ene grete nauye sente brother belyn shold yeld yen lande wife folke castelles also elles wold destroie lande belyn drade thyng manace wold thyng done said wherfore brenne come folke fought belyn brenne discomfited folke slayne hym selfe fledde xij fraunce belyn brennes brother wet tho yorke toke counceill myght done kyng gutlagh kyng gutlagh prof ed become man holde hi lande hym yelding yere thousand pounde siluer euermore sikernesse couenaunt behold gutlagh shold bring good hostage shold done homage folke yit shold swere vpon boke couenantz shold neuer bene broke ne falsed pbelyn tho counceill folke graunted hym axyng gutlagh become man belyn vnderfeng hym homage othe writing couenants vpon couenants kyng gutlagh nome samye folke went then turned ayen denma c euermore couenats holden truage payed til tyme honelos kyng denmarc also lande thurgh wif gildeburgh spoused wa right heir lande pthis belyn duelled tho pee romayns come lande conquere truage thurgh strength haue kyng kyng gynder armager brother gadred grete hoost yfere briton yafe bataille emperour claudius queld romayns grete plente emperour afterward one called hamon sawe hir peple ware fast slayue preuelich cast way owne armes toke armes dede briton armed hym armure come bataille kyng said maner sir beye good hert goddis loue romayns bene yone enemy anone shull slayne discomfited euerychon kyng yaf kepe ne reward speche encheson armes vpon hym went bene briton traitour euer helde hym next kyng preuelich vnder shuldres armes smote kyng wher yaf hem contre forleten myght duelle thidder went duelled hir lyfes tyme ixc men hem mo lefte bataill hir go nour prince called berynger anon bigan toune myght duell haue restorte let calle toune richely auaunce traitour coppa put vpon hym abbyt religion let shaue hym brode croune come kynges court said wolde hele kyng maladie tho said traitour coppa vn kyng sir ben good comfort shall yeue yow medicine ye shull swete anon right lusten sleep haue good rest traitour yaf hym suche poyson sleep anone right died slepyng traitour said wold gone oute felde till waked scaped away man hym suspection encheson abbyt clothed also brode croune kynges men wyst dede becomen wonder sory fast sought traitour myght fynde hym coppa turued ayene host frowhens come pwhen aurilambros dede sterre morne seyne clere light bought beme seyne hede horrible dragon calxviij kyng aurilambros thus dede enpoisened wynchestre amorne dede aboute tyme prime ther seyne st rre grete clere beme sterre brighter tha sonne bouyt beem aped dragos hede mouth come ij huge lightes bright fire brennyg pand one beme till toward fraunce straught ouer see thidder ward pand beem come vij bemes full clere longe liyt fire pthis sterne se n many man none hem wyst betokened pvter kynges brother walys host britos saw sterre grete light yaf wondred ther gretly myyt betoken let call merlyn praied telle myyt betoke pof betokenyng sterre pcalxix merlyn saw sterre behelde hym loge tyme sithene qnoke wept tenderly said allas allas noble kyng worthy dede pand yowe vnderstonde aurilambros brother enpoysened see well sterre self betokened hede dragon seyn bought beem self shall kyng regne beem stot towardes est vnderstonde ye shall gete sone shall conquere frau ce landes ben lougyng croun fraunce shall worthier kyng honour euer auncestres pand beem streyght toward irland betokened ye shall geten doughter shall quene irland pand vij bemes betokened shall haue vij sone euery hem shall kyng regne mochell honour abyde ye lenger goth yeue bataille enemy fyghted hem boldely ye shull ouercome hem haue victorie pvter thanked hertely merlyn nome men went toward enymie foughten gedre mortaly discomfited enymies destroied hym self quelled passent vortigers sone pand briton queld guillomer kyng irland men pand vter anon bataill toke way toward wynchestre done etier aurilambros kyng thas wat brother pbut tho body borne stonhenge mochel honour done made remebrauce briton ther ware slayn thurgh treson engist day shold haue bene accorded place entered aurilambros seconde yerr regne wurshipp myyt belongen kyug who soule god haue mercy pof vter pendragon wherfor called ye shall ouer take grete loue igerne erle cornewailles wife calxx deth aurilambros vter brother crouned regned well worthely remembraunce dragon liked let make two dragon thurgh counceill briton one bore hym whenne went bataille othir abide wynchestre bisshoppes chyrche pand encheson called euer vter pendragon pand otta engistes sone commended litell vter made newe kyng ayens hym began meue werre ordeyned grete companie frendes kynne os brother take land humber vn yorke tho yorke helde strongely agayne hem nold suffre hem come toune nothir yelde cite hem beseged toune anone right yafe ther stronge assaute cite hem kepte well strongly pand vter herde ther come thidder grete power helpe rescue toune put away siege yafe stronge bataille otta companie hem defended well myght last discomfited part hem aueld otta os taken put prison london pand vter hym selfe dnelled yorke went london ester sueng wolde bere corone holde solempne fest let sompne erles baron shold come fest tho wyfes sholde bring hem also feste comen kynges co maundement commaunded fest richely holden worthely set mete estate erle gorloys corne waill igerne wyfe seten alther next kyng kyng saw fairnesse lady ranysshed hir beaute ofte made hir nyce semblant lokyng laughyng last erle ceyued ue lokyng laughyng loue bitwene hem aroos p fro toble wrath toke wyfe called knyghtes went then wrath withoute takyng bene kyng kyng anone sent hym shold come ayene goo then despite hym pand erle wold come ayene maner wyse pwherfor kyng full wroth wrath hym deffied anone beseged castell ther duelled xv dayes neuer myght spede euer thought vpon ygerne vpon hir laid moche loue nyst last called hym knyght called vlfyn priue hym told hym conseill axed hym best done psir qd dothe send aft r merlyn telle yowe best couceill man lyuyng merlyn anone sent come kyng kyng told hym wyll psir qd merlyn shall done moche thurgh crafte shall make yowe come nyyt castell erles chambirlayne eche hem transfigured othir likenesse pand merlyn done said kyng sir qd nowe mowe ye gone sodeynly castell tyntagell axen entre ther haue wyll kyng toke priuely host go ne lede knyyt moche loued nome way toward castell hym vlfin chambirlayn merlyn pand come thidder portier went bene lord tyme come go ledde pthe kyng wet bedde igerne erles wyf hir wyll bigate vpon hir sone called arthur pvpon mor noble myghty kyng nome leue lady went ayen host pand nyght kyng lay ygerne bedde fere erles wif kynges men yeuen stronge assaut castell erle men manly hem defended last befell atte assaute erle hym selfe slayne castell taken pand kyng anone turned ayene tyntagell spoused igerne mochel honour made hir quene sone tyme come shold deliuered bere child sone called arthur gate hir doughter called amya whan come age nobely maried noble baron called aloth lord leon pwhen vter longe tyme regned ther come vpon hym grete sikenesse sorwe pand mene tyme tho kepe otta engistes sone os brother tho prison men let hem gone grete yiftes hem yaf wente hem pand tho two bretheren ascaped come ayen hir owne contre ordeyned hem grete hoost grete poer begone eftsones vpon kyng phow kyng vter chese aloth kepe land britaigne while sike moche myght sikenesse capitulo septuagesimosecundo moche kyng vter sike myght helpe hym selfe ordeyned aloth sone eleyne tho chosen wardeyne chiueteyne sore let put hem lytter hoost amonges folke pand lad hym veroloyne tho faire cite ther seint albone martred cite destroied paynyms thurgh werre thidder sence otta os hir peple entred toune let make fase yates ther halde hem kyng come hem beseged made stronge assauce tho within manlich hem defended pthe kyng let ordeyne gonne engynes breke walles walles stronge thyng myght hem mysdoo potta peple grete despite kyng byggyng lytter hem beseged token counceill amonges hem stonde vp morwe come oute yeue bataille kyng diden bataille bothe otta os slayne tho othir ascaped lyue fled scotland made colegryne hir chyuetay ne saxon lyue ascaped fro bataile brough ten ayene grete strength amoges hem seyden yf kyng vter dede shold well conquere land amonges thought enpoisen kyng ordeyned men done dede yaf hem yiftes grete plente thyng done ordeyned hem thidderward ther kyng ducllyng clo thed hem pouerwede better spede hir lither purpose nothelees hir falsenesse queyntize myght ne come nygh kyng pbut last aspied kyng drank none othir licour water clere well nygh besides pand thees fals traitours vpon day preuelich wente well put therin poysen water enpoisened anone kyng dronke wat began swell sone died many dronken water deide also pand anone falsenesse aspied foll toune let stoppe well euermore pwhen kyng dede folke hym stonhenge grete solempnite bisshops baron beried hym beside aur lambros brother turned ayene tho euerichon lot sende arthur sone made hym kyng land moch reuereuce fadres deth xvij yere regne phow arthur sone vter crouned fadres deth drofe colegrine saxones cheldrik almayne oute land calxxiij arthur made kyng lad yong age xv yere faire bolde doubty body meke folke good cour oi large spendyng made hym welbeloued among men ther nede pand began regne swore saxon neure shold haue pee ne rest till driue hem oute lande let assemble grate hoost faught colegrine tyme otta dede saxon mayntened colkgrine discomfited fledde vij yorke toke toune ther helde hym pand kyng beseged toune bnt myght thyng spede toune stronge withynne kepte toune well orpedly pand ment yme colegriue let toune bladulf fled hym selfe cheldryke kyng almayne haue hym socour kyng assembled grete power come arriued scotland vc shippes arthur wyst tydyng nat poer strength ynowe fight ayens cheldryk let bene fie e wente ot london sente anone lettres kyng litell britaigne callyd token hir way euen ni hol cheldrik beseged nouzt yit taken pand come vpon cheldrik vpon peple wyst ther hem egrely assailled kyng chel drik meyny defended hem manly hir poer kyng arthur men quelled many saxon neuer er say ne suche slaughter pand cheldrik men left alyue fledden waye pand arthur hem poursued drofe hem wode myght ferthir passe cheldrik sawe well brought moche disese hem yolden arthur maner wyse sholde take hir hors hir armure must gone fote hir shippes wolde gone hir owne lande neuer come yen land vpon assurance thyng yeuen hym good hostage pand arthur coceill graunted thyng resseyued hostage vpon wet hir shippes pand hie see wyll chaged deuel wolde retourned hir nauye come yene lande arrined tenesse went hir shippes nome land clene robbed moche peple slew token armure myght fynde went forth till comen bathe men toune shitten fast hir yates wolde suffre hem come yn toune defended hem well orpedly ayens hem phowe arthur yafe bataill saxones come ayen beseged toune bathe hem ouercome capitulo lxxiiij arthur herde tydynge let honge anone hostage lefte hoel britayne nepheu ke e marche ward scotland half peple selfe wet helpe reskew toune bathe come thidder yaf stronge bataill cheldrik queld al peple man myyt hym withstond ne endure vn stroke swerd pand ther bothe slayne colegryne bladud brother pand cheldryk fledde then wolde haue gone shippes arthur regne england land sholde ende calxxv sir qd merlyn yere incarnacion ihesu criste mccxv shall come lambe oute wynchestre shall haue white tonge trewe lippes shall haue writen herte holynesse pthis lambe shall make many goddes house shall haue pee lyfe shall make one fairest place world tyme shall nat fully made ende pand ende lyfe wolf strang land shall moche harme sorwe thurgh werre ende lambe shall mastir thurgh helpe rede fox shall come oute northwest hym shall ouercome wolfe shall die water tyme lambe shall lyue ne shall die phi sede shall strange land land shall withoute gouernour litell tyme shall come dragon melled mercy wodenesse shall haue erd goot shall yeue englond shade shall kepe land colde hete one scot shall sette wyke othir london shall enbrace babitacions shall open mouth toward walis trembling hidour mouth eres shall strech toward many habitacions contries breth shall full swete strange lande pand hiz tyme shall river renne blode brayne shall make place land walles sh lle done moch harme vn seed tyme pthen shall ther come peple northwest regne shall lad thurgh wikked hare dragon shall done croune kyng afterwad shall lee ouer see without comyng ayen drede dragon pand tyme sone shall reede blode shull see thurgh world shall betoken grete pestilence deth folk thurgh dent swerde peple shall ben fadreles till tyme dragon shall die thurgh hare shall meue ayens hym werre vn end lyfe shall fully bene ended tyme dragon shall hold tyme best body world shall die besides march strange lande lande shall duelle fadreles without good gouernour shall deth ile shepey vn hauen marall pwherfor allas shall commune songe fadrelees folk shull ouerlynen land destroied dragon shall come goot kar shall haue horne berde siluer ther shall come nostrell adomp shall betoken hunger grete deth peple mochel lande begynnyng regne shall wasted pthis goot shall go ouer feaunce shall opene flour lyfe deth tyme ther shall arise egle corne waille shall haue fethers golde pride shall pere lande shall despise lordes blode shall flee shamfully bere gauersech shull made brigges men vpon costes see stone shull fall fro castelles many othir tounes shull made playne tyme shall seme bere shall brenne bataille shall done vpon armes see feld ordeyned sheld bataille shall die many white heedes wherfor bataill shall called white bataille pand forsaid bere shall done goot mochel harme shall come oute southwest blood shall goot lese moche land till tyme shendshipp shall hym come shall cloth hym lyon skynne shall wynne lost ther peple shall come oute northwest shall make goot sore adrad shall venge enemy thurgh counceill two owles first shall ill bene vn done olde oule shall wende certayne tyme shall come ayene land pthese two owles shullen grete harme many shall counceill goot shall arere werre ayens forsaid bere last goot owles shall come burton vp trent shull wende ouer drede bere shall flee aswan hym fro companie burton toward north ther shull bene hard shour swan shall slayne forwe bere taken heded alther next nest shall stonde vpon broken brngge sonn shall cast hir bemes many shall hym seke vertu fro shall come pin shall die sorwe care peple land many landes shull bene hym bolder afterward tho two owles shulle moche harme forsaid flour lyse hir shull lede distresse shall passe fraunce make pee bitwene goot flour delise ther shall duelle till thurgh world boor holynesse fersenesse nobilesse mekenesse shall done mesurably shall haue done vn burgh ihrlm shall whett teth vpon yates paris vpon iiij landes spaigne shall tremble drede gastoyne fullfylled good boor shall come lambe shall haue foot leed hede bra hert loppe swynes skyn harde tyme lade shall bene pee fyrst yere regne shall make cite world shall speke ther pthis lambe shall leue tyme grete part lande thurgh hidons wolfe shall recouer yeue lordshipp egle line egle shall well gouerne till tyme pride shall hym ouergone allas sorwe shall deye brother suerd shall lande fall pfor nowe ye haue done v ouercome loue god suffre v lyue haueth mercy cristen peple beleuen crist ye done pwhen kyng arthur herde sorwe pite hem yaf hem lyfe lymme fyll doune fete bicome liegmen toke hem come yn xij eldren men age richely araied courtoisely salued kyng said come rome sent messagiers fro emour toke hym lre thus moche vnderstond pgretly v mervaileth arthure thou art one hardie eien thy hede make open werre contake ayens v rome owen worlde deme thou hast neu neuer yet biforne tyme proued ne assaied stregth romayns therfor thou shalt litell tyme iulius cesar conquerd land
